Carnegie Mellon University School of Music Subscribe Carnegie Mellon Chamber Series: Jeremy Denk @ CMU! Wednesday, March 26, 2025 from 07:30 pm to 09:30 pm Event Details WHEN Wednesday, March 26, 2025 from 07:30 pm to 09:30 pm WHERE Kresge Theatre, College of Fine Arts at 5000 Forbes Avenue Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania, United States, 15213 COST This is a free event! Register CONTACT School of Music Box Office 412-268-2383 412-268-2383 Categories: Concerts Tags: Chamber Series Description Tickets Organizer Venue Description Carnegie Mellon Chamber Series: Jeremy Denk @ CMU! The Carnegie Mellon University Chamber Series brings together members of the CMU Faculty and Pittsburgh Symphony Orchestra for outstanding music making in an intimate space. Program: Ludwig van Beethoven Piano Sonata in A-flat major Unsuk Chin Complete Piano Etudes Jeremy Denk, piano Ludwig van Beethoven Piano Trio in E-Flat Major Jeremy Denk, piano David McCarroll, violin Angela Park, cello Cost: Free and open to the public; Tickets required. Cost and Tickets Cost & Tickets This is a free event!
